# Text Elements
What happens when we type a url into a Browser


https://www.google.com/api/seach?q=home ^j6A1lBPI

Scheme
Which protocal we are using to connect 
 ^pqtlyp8D

Flow of how things happen ^ZcXM53QU

Dns Resultion ^nHzYNd7s

Path ^F4yMPff8

Dns Lookup happens here which means that the Browser site url that we type is being mapped to the
ip adress of the Server machine 

DNS information is heavily cached 

Once the ip address is mapped since the ip address of the websites does not change much this ip address
is cached by the browser so that when the user makes a request again it is directly mapped instead
of doing a dns lookup ^MzSyrqtQ

This may sound like a small task but it requires many servers to do this  ^YStajKUv

Tcp connection ^2Pf98MZx

Browser Estalished a TCP connection with the Server After that the  ^Kb6Z8iIS

Browser ^J8TR1QK3

TCP ^TVXE3SEg

Server ^r384VZAO

Load balancer ^EhZ6u4ST

Server1 ^DsABTIzS

Serevr2 ^1b7p3DzU

Server3 ^UnYJLE3o

This is a whole different Process what we need to discuss after words ^tkehsRmH

DNS Lookup ^xM6LvzjX

OS also caches the Dns information ^OPuqjkOk

Sending the request ^bdCpE7tO

Makes the http Request Http is a Protocol
Further investigatewhy does Protocols  Exist?

BR0wser sends a a http request to the server with  a http Packet 

Packet contains the meta data ^XGaMUfBK

Server Receives the requst ^v79HYUlx

Response is typically downloaded by the browser 

and the Browser takes the response body and parses and displayes the files and makes subsequent api calls 
if required ^iAWyZ8fm

Server parses the Packet With the Header and gets the basic meta info ^lgvRnAjp

and understands what needs to be done  
Server loads the file form the local disk space and serves it to the client as 
Response ^w5Nn6Mb5
